   BhG 2.1	Bhu 2.1

   sthita-prajña-lakṣaṇāni mumukṣu-kartavyatayā kathitāni | samprati	sTita--prajQa--lakzaNAni mumukzu-kartavya-tayA kaTitAni | samprati
   karma-yoga-phala-bhūtāṃ sāṅkhya-niṣṭhāṃ stuvann upasaṃharati eṣeti | eṣā	karma--yoga--Pala--BUtAm sAFKya--nizWAm stuvan upasaMharati ezA-iti | ezA
   sthita-prajña-lakṣaṇa-vyājena kathitā | eṣā te 'bhihitā sāṅkhye buddhir	sTita--prajQa--lakzaNa--vyAjena kaTitAH | ezA te aBihitA sAFKye budDiH-
   iti ca prāg uktā sthitir niṣṭhā	iti ca prAk uktA sTitiH nizWA
   sarva-karma-saṃnyāsa-pūrvaka-paramātma-jñāna-lakṣaṇā brāhmī brahma-viṣayā	sarva-karma--saMnyAsa--pUrvaka-param-Atma--jQAna--lakzaNA brAhmI brahma-vizayA
   | he pārtha ! enāṃ sthitiṃ prāpya yaḥ kaścid api pnar na vimuhyati | na hi	| he pArTa ! enAm sTitim prApya yaH kaScid api pnar na vimuhyati | na hi
   jñāna-bādhitasyājñānasya punaḥ sambhavo 'sti anāditvenotpatty-asambhavāt |	jQAna-bADitasya-ajQAnasya punar samBavaH asti anAdi-tvena-utpatti--asamBavAt |
   asyāṃ sthitāv anta-kāle 'pi antye 'pi vaayasi sthitvā brahma-nirvāṇaṃ	asyAm sTitO anta-kAle api antye api vaayasi sTitvA brahma--nirvANam
   brahmaṇi nirvāṇaṃ nirvṛttiṃ brahma-rūpaṃ nirvāṇam iti vā | ṛcchati	brahmaNi nirvANam nirvRttim brahma-rUpam nirvANam iti vA | RcCati
   gacchaty abhedena | kim u vaktavyaṃ yo bramacaryād eva saṃnyasya	gacCati aBedena | kim u vaktavyam yaH brama-caryAt eva saMnyasya
   yāvaj-jīvam asyāṃ brāhmyāṃ sthitāv avatiṣṭhate sa brahma-nirvāṇam	yAvaj-jIvam asyAm brAhmyAm sTitO avatizWate sa brahma--nirvANam
   ṛcchatīty api-śabdārthaḥ ||72||	RcCati-iti api-Sabda-arTaH ||72||
   iti	iti
   śrīmat-paramahaṃsa-parivrājakācārya-śrī-viśveśvara-sarasvatī-pāda-śiṣya-śrī-madhusūdana-sarasvatī-viracitāyāṃ	SrImat-paramahaMsa--parivrAjaka-AcArya--SrI--viSveSvara--sarasvatI--pAda--Sizya--SrI--maDusUdana--sarasvatI--viracitAyAm
   śrīmad-bhagavad-gītā-gūḍhārtha-dīpikāyām sarva-gītārtha-sūtraṇaṃ nāma	SrI-mat--Bagavat--gItA--gUXa-arTa-dIpikAyAm sarva--gIta-arTa-sUtraNam nAma
   dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||2||	dvitIyaH aDyAyaH ||2||
   viśvanāthaḥ : upasaṃharati eṣeti | brāhmī brahma-prāpikā | anta-kāle	viSvanATaH : upasaMharati ezA-iti | brAhmI brahma-prApikAH | anta-kAle
   mṛtyu-samaye 'pi | kiṃ punar ābālyam ||72||	mRtyu--samaye api | kim punar AbAlyam ||72||
   jñānaṃ karma ca vispaṣṭam aspaṣṭaṃ bhaktim uktavān |	jQAnam karma ca vispazwam aspazwam Baktim uktavAn |
   ataevāyam adhyāyaḥ śrī-gītā-sūtram ucyate ||	ataeva-ayam aDyAyaH SrI--gItA--sUtram ucyate ||
   iti sārārtha-varṣiṇyāṃ harṣiṇyāṃ bhakta-cetasām |	iti sAra-arTa-varziNyAm harziNyAm Bakta--cetasAm |
   śrī-gītāsu dvitīyo 'yaṃ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||2||	SrI--gItAsu dvitIyaH ayam saFgataH saFgataH satAm ||2||
   baladevaḥ : sthita-prajñatāṃ stauti eṣeti | brāhmī brahma-prāpikā |	baladevaH : sTita--prajQa-tAm stOti ezA-iti | brAhmI brahma-prApikA |
   anta-kāle carame vayasi | kiṃ punar ākaumāraṃ brahma ṛcchati labhate |	anta-kAle carame vayasi | kim punar AkOmAram brahma RcCati laBate |
   nirvāṇam amṛta-rūpaṃ tat pradam ity arthaḥ | nanu tasyāṃ sthitaḥ kathaṃ	nirvANam amRta--rUpam tat pradam iti arTaH | nanu tasyAm sTitaH kaTam
   brahma prāpnoti | tat-prāptes tad-bhakti-hetukatvād iti ced ucyate |	brahma prApnoti | tat--prApteH tad--Bakti--hetuka-tvAt iti ced ucyate |
   tasyās tad-bhakti-hetukatvāt tad-bhakti-hetutvāc ca tat-prāpakateti ||72||	tasyAH tad--Bakti--hetuka-tvAt tad--Bakti-hetu-tvAt ca tat--prApaka-tA-iti ||72||
   niṣkāma-karmabhir jñānī harim eva smaran bhavet |	nizkAma--karmaBiH jQAnI harim eva smaran Bavet |
   anyathā vighna eveti dvitīyo 'dhyāya-nirṇayaḥ ||	anyaTA viGnaH eva-iti dvitIyaH aDyAya--nirNayaH ||
   iti śrīmad-bhagavad-gītopaniṣad-bhāṣye dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ |	iti SrI-mat--Bagavat--gIta-upanizad--BAzye dvitIyaH aDyAyaH |
